CREATE TABLE Protein (protein_id INT PRIMARY KEY, protein_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, protein_sequence TEXT NOT NULL)

CREATE TABLE Gene (gene_id INT PRIMARY KEY, gene_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL, gene_sequence TEXT NOT NULL)</t><s>alter table experiment drop column result</s>
